# PRADY OS ÔÇö SOVEREIGN EDITION

> *The machine owns execution. The Sovereign owns strategic authorization.*

PRADY OS is a Linux-based autonomous AI operating system in which a constellation of
specialist agents collectively governs the machine with administrator-level authority.
The human is elevated out of routine operation and positioned as the **Sovereign** who
approves or rejects projects, strategic initiatives, constitutional changes, and
irreversible high-impact actions.

The CLI is fully hidden. Agents own the terminal plane. The Sovereign sees only the
**Governance Chamber** ÔÇö proposals, outcomes, incidents, approvals.

This is **Phase 0** of the build. It establishes the substrate: the hidden command
runner (TITAN OPS), the health telemetry mesh (WARDEN GRID), the orchestration kernel
(IMPERIUM), and the governance terminal seed (AURORA THRONE).

---

## The Three Laws

1. **Autonomous Execution** ÔÇö all reversible and policy-compliant operational work is
   executed by the machine without routine human intervention.
2. **Sovereign Approval of Strategic Direction** ÔÇö projects, strategic initiatives,
   constitutional changes, and irreversible actions cross the Sovereign boundary.
3. **Transparent Power** ÔÇö broad operational authority is granted only because every
   significant action is observable, attributable, explainable, logged, and
   rollback-aware.

## Approval Boundary

Only the following require human approval:

- New projects surfaced by ORACLE
- Major strategic or architectural shifts
- Irreversible destructive actions on high-value state
- Data exfiltration beyond trusted boundaries
- Constitutional rule changes

Everything else executes autonomously within policy envelopes.

---

## Core Components

| Component | Role | Plane |
|-----------|------|-------|
| `pradyos.titan_ops` | Hidden command runner ÔÇö admin-grade execution fabric | Execution |
| `pradyos.warden_grid` | Real-time health telemetry and incident detection | Recovery / Substrate |
| `pradyos.imperium` | Task queue, state machine, policy classifier, DAG | Orchestration |
| `pradyos.aurora_throne` | Sovereign Governance Chamber (terminal UI) | Experience |
| `pradyos.core` | Shared substrate ÔÇö audit log, constitution, bus, IDs | Foundational |
| `pradyos.oracle` | AI reasoning, planning, autonomous proposal loop | Intelligence |
| `pradyos.campaign` | Campaign engine ÔÇö multi-step DAG execution | Orchestration |
| `pradyos.proving_ground` | Constitutional admission gate | Safety |
| `pradyos.memory_citadel` | Persistent vector memory | Memory |
| `pradyos.sovereign` | Sovereign Web UI + CLI + REPL | Experience |

The raw CLI is never the user surface. `pradyos-throne` is the only sanctioned
entrypoint.

---

## Build Instructions

### Local development (no privilege escalation)

```bash
git clone <repo> pradyos
cd pradyos
python3.11 -m venv .venv
source .venv/bin/activate
pip install -e ".[dev]"
pytest -v
```

Launch the governance terminal:

```bash
python -m pradyos.service          # starts all daemons in-process
# in another terminal ÔÇö but only this one, and only this surface, is sanctioned:
python -m pradyos.aurora_throne    # the Throne
```

### Docker dev environment

```bash
docker compose up --build
```

This brings up TITAN OPS, WARDEN GRID, and IMPERIUM as separate containers and
exposes the WARDEN GRID JSON API on `localhost:9701`.

### Systemd deployment (Sovereign build)

```bash
sudo cp deploy/systemd/*.service /etc/systemd/system/
sudo systemctl daemon-reload
sudo systemctl enable --now pradyos-titan.service \
                            pradyos-warden.service \
                            pradyos-imperium.service
# Throne is launched on Sovereign login, not as a service.
```

---

## Repo Layout

```
pradyos/
ÔöťÔöÇÔöÇ core/            # shared substrate
ÔöťÔöÇÔöÇ titan_ops/       # hidden command runner (Plane 2)
ÔöťÔöÇÔöÇ warden_grid/     # health telemetry + incident mesh (Plane 1/9)
ÔöťÔöÇÔöÇ imperium/        # orchestration kernel (Plane 3)
ÔööÔöÇÔöÇ aurora_throne/   # governance terminal (Plane 10)
docs/                # architecture + API contracts
deploy/              # systemd units + Dockerfile
tests/               # pytest suite
var/                 # audit log + checkpoint state (gitignored)
```

---

## Status

**Phase 7 ÔÇö Complete.** All 35 test modules green (82.7 s). Audit hooks,
metrics hooks, retry hooks, config watcher, REPL extensions, and deploy
pipeline are provably wired.

**Phase 8 ÔÇö Complete.** All 37 test modules green. ORACLE autonomous proposal
loop and Campaign Ôćö Proving Ground admission bridge provably wired.

**Phase 9 ÔÇö Complete.** All 37 test modules green. Four deliverables:
- Ôťů 9A: Production systemd units for **all five services** ÔÇö `pradyos-titan`,
  `pradyos-warden`, `pradyos-imperium`, `pradyos-oracle` (new), and
  `pradyos-admission` (new). All units restart on failure, log to journald,
  and carry a full set of systemd sandboxing directives (`NoNewPrivileges`,
  `ProtectSystem=strict`, `PrivateTmp`, `PrivateDevices`,
  `ProtectKernelModules`, `ProtectControlGroups`, `RestrictNamespaces`,
  `LockPersonality`, `MemoryDenyWriteExecute`, `SystemCallFilter`). Dependency
  ordering: WARDEN + TITAN Ôćĺ IMPERIUM Ôćĺ ORACLE Ôćĺ ADMISSION.
- Ôťů 9B: Docker hardening ÔÇö `deploy/Dockerfile` upgraded to Python 3.12,
  `COPY --chown=pradyos` throughout. `deploy/docker-compose.yml` gains
  `oracle` and `admission` services wired with healthchecks
  (`/oracle/status` and
import-probe respectively), plus fleet-wide
  `cap_drop: [ALL]`, `security_opt: no-new-privileges:true`,
  `read_only: true`, `tmpfs: /tmp`, and a single named volume
  `pradyos-var` for audit log + state persistence. Secrets managed via
  `deploy/secrets.env` (template at `deploy/secrets.env.example`).
- Ôťů 9C: `tests/test_deploy.py` extended with 28 new assertions covering
  new systemd units, Docker hardening directives, oracle/admission
  service definitions, and healthcheck presence. All 37 modules remain green.
- Ôťů 9D: README updated.

**Phase 10 ÔÇö Complete.** All 38 test modules green (28.7 s). Redis
inter-process bus live across Docker and systemd planes:
- Ôťů 10A: `pradyos/core/redis_bus.py` ÔÇö `RedisBus` drop-in replacement for
  `EventBus` using redis-py Pub/Sub. A daemon thread polls
  `pubsub.get_message()` and dispatches to registered callbacks. Regular
  topics use `SUBSCRIBE`; the wildcard `"*"` topic uses `PSUBSCRIBE("*")`.
  Subscriber faults are isolated; unsubscribe triggers `UNSUBSCRIBE` /
  `PUNSUBSCRIBE` when the last handler is removed.
- Ôťů 10B: `pradyos/core/bus.py` ÔÇö `get_bus()` factory updated. When
  `PRADYOS_BUS_BACKEND=redis`, returns `RedisBus`; otherwise the existing
  in-process `EventBus`. Zero call-site changes.
- Ôťů 10C: `deploy/docker-compose.yml` ÔÇö `redis:7-alpine` service added with
  a `redis-cli ping` healthcheck and a named volume (`pradyos-redis`). All
  application services gain `PRADYOS_BUS_BACKEND=redis`,
  `PRADYOS_REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379/0`, and `depends_on: [redis]`.
- Ôťů 10D: All six `deploy/systemd/*.service` files (`pradyos-titan`,
  `pradyos-warden`, `pradyos-imperium`, `pradyos-oracle`, `pradyos-admission`,
  `pradyos-throne`) updated with
  `Environment=PRADYOS_BUS_BACKEND=redis` and
  `Environment=PRADYOS_REDIS_URL=redis://127.0.0.1:6379/0`.
- Ôťů 10E: `tests/test_redis_bus.py` ÔÇö 16 tests using `fakeredis` (no real
  Redis server required). Covers pub/sub, wildcard, unsubscribe, fault
  isolation, payload round-trip, and `get_bus()` factory.
- Ôťů 10F: `pyproject.toml` dev deps extended with `redis>=5.0` and
  `fakeredis>=2.0`. `deploy/secrets.env.example` documents new env vars.


**Phase 11 ÔÇö Complete.** All 41 test modules green. Autonomous self-healing live:
- Ôťů 11A: `pradyos/imperium/self_heal.py` ÔÇö `SelfHealEngine` with `heal()`,
  `is_quarantined()`, `release_quarantine()`, `quarantine_list()`. Loads
  latest `SnapshotStore` entry as rollback reference, quarantines offending
  tasks in-memory + persisted to `var/state/quarantine.json`, publishes
  `system.self_heal` bus event (WARDEN auto-raises incident via `system.*`
  wildcard), and writes a structured audit entry.
- Ôťů 11B: `pradyos/imperium/kernel.py` ÔÇö `Imperium.rollback()` method added;
  `Imperium._self_heal_hook()` callback wired into `RecoveryCore.on_exhausted`
  so any task that exhausts its retry budget is healed autonomously.
  `pradyos/imperium/recovery.py` extended with `on_exhausted` callback slot.
- Ôťů 11C: `pradyos/imperium/exceptions.py` ÔÇö `TaskNotFound` custom exception.
- Ôťů 11D: `tests/test_self_heal.py` ÔÇö 22 tests: `HealResult` correctness,
  quarantine persistence, `is_quarantined`, `release_quarantine`, bus events,
  audit entries, kernel integration (auto-heal on dead-letter), idempotency,
  snapshot reference, multi-task quarantine, and WARDEN notification.
- Ôťů 11E: `scripts/prove.py` updated; README Phase Map updated.

**Phase 16 ÔÇö Complete.** All 49 test modules green. OTel-compatible telemetry pipeline ÔÇö every significant OS event emits a structured span stored in a ring buffer and queryable via API:
- Ôťů 16A: `pradyos/core/telemetry.py` ÔÇö `TelemetrySpan` dataclass (span_id, trace_id, parent_id, name, service, start_ts, end_ts, status, attributes) with `duration_ms()` and `to_dict()`. `TelemetryCollector` ring-buffer (collections.deque maxlen=500) with `start_span()`, `finish_span()`, `record()` (one-shot), `get_spans(limit, service, status)` returning most-recent-first, `clear()`, and `__len__()`. Thread-safe via threading.Lock. Auto-generates UUID4 hex span_id and trace_id. `finish_span()` returns None for unknown span_id ÔÇö never raises.
- Ôťů 16B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ÔÇö `GET /api/v1/telemetry` endpoint wired via optional `telemetry` param in `create_app()`. Query params: `limit` (int, default 100, max 500), `service` (str|None), `status` (str|None). Returns `{"spans": [...], "count": int}`. Safe empty response `{"spans": [], "count": 0}` when telemetry not injected.
- Ôťů 16C: `tests/test_telemetry.py` ÔÇö 20 unit tests covering start_span status/id generation/explicit trace_id/append, finish_span status/end_ts/merge/unknown-id, record default/duration_ms/error, get_spans list/limit/service filter/status filter/order, clear, maxlen eviction, and duration_ms None vs computed.
- Ôťů 16D: `tests/test_telemetry_web.py` ÔÇö 10 FastAPI TestClient tests: HTTP 200, spans/count keys, spans is list, count==len(spans), limit param, service filter, status filter, count reflects filter, no-telemetry empty response.
- Ôťů 16E: `scripts/prove.py` updated with both new test modules (49 total).
- Ôťů 16F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 17 planned.

**Phase 17 ÔÇö Complete.** All 51 test modules green. Sovereign Memory Graph ÔÇö a knowledge graph layer where the OS stores facts, relationships, and inferences about campaigns, tasks, and system state ÔÇö queryable via API and visualised in the Aurora Throne TUI:
- Ôťů 17A: `pradyos/core/memorygraph.py` ÔÇö `GraphNode` and `GraphEdge` dataclasses with `to_dict()`. `SovereignMemoryGraph` with bounded storage (maxnodes/maxedges), LRU-by-age eviction, `add_node()`, `add_edge()`, `get_node()`, `get_edge()`, `neighbours(relation=None)`, `query_nodes(kind, label)` sorted newest-first, `remove_node()` cascading edge removal, `remove_edge()`, `stats()`, `clear()`. Thread-safe via `threading.Lock`. Auto-generates UUID4 hex ids.
- Ôťů 17B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ÔÇö `GET /api/v1/graph/stats` returns `{"nodes": int, "edges": int}`; `POST /api/v1/graph/nodes` body `{kind, label, node_id?, attributes?}` returns new node dict; `GET /api/v1/graph/nodes?kind&label&limit` returns `{"nodes": [...], "count": int}`; `GET /api/v1/graph/nodes/{node_id}/neighbours?relation` returns `{"neighbours": [...], "count": int}`. Wired via new `graph` param in `create_app()`. Safe empty responses when graph not injected.
- Ôťů 17C: `tests/test_memorygraph.py` ÔÇö 20 unit tests covering add_node kind/label/auto-id/explicit-id/stats, add_edge fields/auto-id/stats, get_node hit/miss, get_edge hit, neighbours basic/relation-filter, query_nodes kind/label filter, remove_node true/false/cascade, remove_edge true/false, maxnodes eviction, and clear.
- Ôťů 17D: `tests/test_memorygraph_web.py` ÔÇö 10 FastAPI TestClient tests: GET stats 200, stats keys, POST node 200, POST required keys, GET nodes 200/shape, count==len after POST, kind filter, GET neighbours 200, neighbours shape/count, no-graph safe empty.

- Ôťů 18B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ÔÇö patched to add optional `ledger` param to `create_app()`; `GET /api/v1/ledger` returns `{entries, count}` with `limit`, `service`, `event` query params; `GET /api/v1/ledger/verify` returns `{valid, count}`. Safe empty responses when no ledger injected.

- Ôťů 19B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ÔÇö patched to add optional `intent` param to `create_app()`; `GET /api/v1/intent/rules` returns `{rules, count}`; `POST /api/v1/intent/rules` body `{rules:[...]}` returns `{loaded}`; `POST /api/v1/intent/suggest` body `{graph_stats, active_campaigns, recent_spans, recent_entries}` returns `{suggestions, count}`. Safe empty responses when no intent injected.

Each section shows up to 20 most-recent items; graceful "No data" when APIs return empty. Auto-refresh every 10 s via `setInterval`. Dark theme consistent with the existing dashboard.

**Phase 21 ÔÇö Complete.** All 59 test modules green. Sovereign Config Hot-Reload ÔÇö a file-watcher that monitors a YAML/JSON config file for changes and hot-reloads intent engine rules, scheduler jobs, and policy rules without restarting the server:
- Ôťů 21A: `pradyos/core/config_hot_reload.py` ÔÇö `ReloadResult` dataclass with `to_dict()`; `ConfigHotReloader` class with `load()`, `start()`, `stop()`, `last_result()`, `status()`. Background daemon thread polls `config_path` every `poll_interval` seconds; reloads on mtime change. Uses `yaml.safe_load` if PyYAML present, falls back to `json.loads` (stdlib-only). Each config section (`intent_rules`, `scheduler_jobs`, `policy_rules`) is optional; missing sections and `None` components are silently skipped. Returns `ReloadResult(success=False, error=ÔÇŽ)` on any exception.
- Ôťů 21B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ÔÇö patched via script to add `config_reloader` param to `create_app()` and two new endpoints: `GET /api/v1/config/status` returns `reloader.status()` (or stub dict when not injected); `POST /api/v1/config/reload` calls `reloader.load()` and returns `result.to_dict()`. `DASHBOARD_HTML` constant untouched.
- Ôťů 21C: `tests/test_config_hot_reload.py` ÔÇö 20 unit tests covering `ReloadResult.to_dict()` keys, `load()` success/failure paths, all three config sections, missing sections, `None` components, file-not-found, invalid JSON, `status()` keys, `_running` transitions, `last_result()` lifecycle, start/stop cycle, changes list type and content.
- Ôťů 21D: `tests/test_config_reload_web.py` ÔÇö 10 FastAPI TestClient tests: HTTP 200 for both endpoints, required response keys, no-reloader stubs, valid-reloader success, error=None on success, config_path reflection, changes list type.
- Ôťů 21E: `scripts/prove.py` updated with both new test modules (59 total).
- Ôťů 21F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 22 planned.

**Phase 23 ÔÇö Complete.** All 63 test modules green. Sovereign Rate-Limit Shield ÔÇö sliding-window, in-memory per-(client_id, endpoint) rate limiter with injectable clock for deterministic testing:
- Ôťů 23A: `pradyos/core/rate_limiter.py` ÔÇö `RateLimitResult` dataclass with `to_dict()` + `RateLimiter` class. Sliding-window counter prunes timestamps older than `window_secs`. `check()` records hits when allowed, does NOT record when denied; returns `retry_after` seconds until reset. `set_rule()` / `get_rules()` for per-endpoint overrides. `reset(client_id, endpoint?)` clears timestamps. `status()` reports active_clients, total_hits, rules. Thread-safe via `threading.Lock`. Zero external dependencies.
- Ôťů 23B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ÔÇö patched via script to add `rate_limiter` optional param to `create_app()` and three new endpoints: `GET /api/v1/ratelimit/status` returns limiter.status() or stub; `POST /api/v1/ratelimit/rules` sets per-endpoint rule; `POST /api/v1/ratelimit/check` evaluates a (client_id, endpoint) pair and returns full RateLimitResult dict. `DASHBOARD_HTML` constant untouched.
- Ôťů 23C: `tests/test_rate_limiter.py` ÔÇö 20 unit tests covering init, check result type, allowed/denied logic, hit recording, sliding window pruning with injectable clock, set_rule/get_rules mutation safety, reset by client and by endpoint, status keys and counts, to_dict keys, retry_after=None/float, 10-hit boundary, cross-endpoint and cross-client independence.
- Ôťů 23D: `tests/test_rate_limit_web.py` ÔÇö 10 FastAPI TestClient tests: HTTP 200 for all endpoints, required keys in responses, allowed=True under limit, stub behaviour when no limiter injected, rule-then-check enforcement.
- Ôťů 23E: `scripts/prove.py` updated with both new test modules (63 total).
- Ôťů 23F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 24 planned.

**Phase 24 ÔÇö Complete.** All 65 test modules green. Sovereign Health Scorecard ÔÇö a composite health score (0ÔÇô100) engine with thread-safe component registry, weighted-average scoring, and A/B/C/D/F grading:
- Ôťů 24A: `pradyos/core/health_scorecard.py` ÔÇö `ComponentScore` and `HealthReport` dataclasses; `HealthScorecard` class with `register()`, `update()` (clamped 0ÔÇô100, auto-registers), `get_report()` (weighted average, grade), `reset()`. Thread-safe via `threading.Lock`.
- Ôťů 24B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched ÔÇö `scorecard` optional param added to `create_app()`; `GET /api/v1/health/score` returns composite report; `POST /api/v1/health/update` accepts name/score/details and calls `scorecard.update()`. Safe empty responses when scorecard not injected.
- Ôťů 24C: `tests/test_health_scorecard.py` ÔÇö 20 unit tests covering init, default report, grade boundaries (A/B/C/D/F), clamping, auto-register, explicit weights, weighted average, `reset()`, `to_dict()` keys, details default, and 50-thread concurrency.
- Ôťů 24D: `tests/test_health_web.py` ÔÇö 10 FastAPI TestClient tests covering GET/POST endpoints, no-scorecard fallbacks (score=100, updated=false), update-then-get round-trip, and grade A/F scenarios.
- Ôťů 24E: `scripts/prove.py` updated to 65 modules.
- Ôťů 24F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 25 planned.

**Phase 25 ÔÇö Complete.** All 67 test modules green. Sovereign Audit Replay Engine ÔÇö a time-travel state reconstructor that replays the append-only audit ledger forward from genesis to reconstruct PradyOS state at any past timestamp:

- Ôťů 25A: `pradyos/core/audit_replay.py` ÔÇö `AuditReplayEngine` with `ReplayEntry` / `ReplaySnapshot` dataclasses; thread-safe via `threading.Lock`; supports external ledger or internal entry list.

**Phase 41 ÔÇö Complete.** All 99 test modules green. Sovereign Heartbeat Loop ÔÇö async background driver that calls `ControlPlane.tick()` on a fixed interval, transforming the OS from on-demand to self-driving; FastAPI startup/shutdown lifecycle hooks auto-start and auto-stop the loop; stdlib + asyncio only:

- Ôťů 41A: `pradyos/core/heartbeat.py` ÔÇö `HeartbeatConfig` (interval_seconds default 5.0, max_ticks optional cap), `HeartbeatLoop` with `start()` (idempotent), `stop()` (graceful with timeout fallback to cancel), `_loop()` (swallows tick exceptions, increments thread-safe counter, stops at max_ticks), `status()`; thread-safe via `threading.Lock` on `tick_count`.
- Ôťů 41B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched ÔÇö `@app.on_event("startup")` auto-calls `heartbeat.start()`, `@app.on_event("shutdown")` calls `heartbeat.stop()`; `GET /api/v1/heartbeat/status` (status dict), `POST /api/v1/heartbeat/stop` (graceful stop) wired into `create_app(heartbeat=...)`. Used `on_event` decorators (not lifespan) to avoid modifying the existing `FastAPI()` call.

**Phase 43 ÔÇö Complete.** All 104 test modules green. **The most important phase.** Without this, the OS cannot safely act autonomously. `GuardrailGate` classifies every intended action by risk (SAFE/LOW/MEDIUM/HIGH/CRITICAL); SAFE/LOW are auto-approved with journal trail; MEDIUM/HIGH/CRITICAL are queued in `ApprovalQueue` for explicit user approval; CRITICAL requires a `reason`. The queue supports approve/reject/expire-stale with TTL fallback. Stdlib only, thread-safe:

- Ôťů 43A: `pradyos/core/guardrail.py` ÔÇö `RiskLevel` enum, `ActionRequest` dataclass (uuid id + to_dict), `GuardrailGate.submit()` (raises ValueError on CRITICAL+no-reason, auto-approves SAFE/LOW with journal record, queues MEDIUM/HIGH/CRITICAL), `status()` (auto_approve_levels + pending queue_size).
- Ôťů 43B: `pradyos/core/approval_queue.py` ÔÇö `ApprovalStatus` enum (PENDING/APPROVED/REJECTED/EXPIRED), `ApprovalEntry` dataclass, `ApprovalQueue` with `add()` (creates PENDING from request), `approve()`/`reject()` (sets resolved_at + resolver_note), `expire_stale()` (TTL sweep), `get()`, `list_by_status()` (sorted by requested_at), `count()` (by status string/enum/None); thread-safe via `threading.Lock`.
- Ôťů 43C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched ÔÇö `GET /api/v1/guardrail/status`, `POST /api/v1/guardrail/submit`, `GET /api/v1/approvals?status=X`, `POST /api/v1/approvals/{id}/approve`, `POST /api/v1/approvals/{id}/reject`, `POST /api/v1/approvals/expire` wired into `create_app(guardrail_gate=..., approval_queue=...)`.
- Ôťů 43D: `tests/test_guardrail.py` ÔÇö 20 unit tests covering ActionRequest fields/serialization, RiskLevel enum, gate init/submit-safe/submit-low/submit-medium-queues/submit-high-queues, CRITICAL-no-reason raises, CRITICAL-with-reason queues, journal integration (auto vs pending), status keys, queue add/approve/reject/expire/count.
- Ôťů 43E: `tests/test_approval_web.py` ÔÇö 10 FastAPI tests (guardrail status no-gate/with-gate, submit safe/medium/invalid-risk, approvals list, approve/reject endpoints, expire count, full submit-HIGHÔćĺapproveÔćĺlist-shows-approved flow).
- Ôťů 43F: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 104 test modules registered.
- Ôťů 43G: README Phase Map updated; Phase 44 planned.

**Phase 52 ÔÇö Complete.** All 122 test modules green. Sovereign DistributedLock ÔÇö TTL-based named mutex; crashed holders cannot deadlock the system because every lock expires automatically; same-holder re-acquire refreshes TTL by design; stdlib only:

- Ôťů 52A: `pradyos/core/distributed_lock.py` ÔÇö `DistributedLock` dataclass with `is_expired()` and `to_dict()`; `LockManager` with `acquire(name, holder_id, ttl=30)` (returns None if held by another non-expired holder; same holder re-acquires by replacing; expired locks can be taken by anyone), `release(name, holder_id)` (True only if caller is non-expired current holder), `refresh()` (extend TTL when caller is current holder and not expired), `is_locked()` (only True if held and not expired), `list_locks()` (excludes expired but doesn't remove them, sorted by acquired_at), `expire_stale()` (removes expired, returns count), `count(include_expired=False)`; thread-safe via `threading.Lock`.
- Ôťů 52B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched ÔÇö `GET /api/v1/locks`, `POST /api/v1/locks` (400 on missing keys, 409 when already held), `POST /api/v1/locks/{name}/refresh` (registered BEFORE delete so the literal `/refresh` doesn't get consumed), `DELETE /api/v1/locks/{name}?holder_id=...` wired into `create_app(lock_manager=...)`.

**Phase 53 ÔÇö Complete.** All 124 test modules green. Sovereign CircuitBreaker ÔÇö per-service failure tracker with CLOSED Ôćĺ OPEN Ôćĺ HALF_OPEN Ôćĺ CLOSED/OPEN state machine; OPEN refuses calls immediately, recovery_timeout transitions to HALF_OPEN, success returns to CLOSED, failure flips back to OPEN; stdlib only:

- Ôťů 53A: `pradyos/core/circuit_breaker.py` ÔÇö `CircuitOpenError`, `BreakerState` dataclass with `to_dict()` (omits internal `half_open_probes` counter), `CircuitBreaker(failure_threshold=5, recovery_timeout=30.0, half_open_max=1)` with `call(name, fn, *args, **kwargs)` (auto-creates state on first use; OPEN check at entry Ôćĺ maybe transition to HALF_OPEN or raise; fn executes OUTSIDE lock so slow handlers don't block other callers; success in CLOSED resets failure_count; success in HALF_OPEN Ôćĺ CLOSED; failure in CLOSED checks threshold Ôćĺ OPEN; failure in HALF_OPEN increments probe count Ôćĺ OPEN at half_open_max), `get_state()`, `reset()` (zeros out all state), `list_breakers()` (sorted by name), `count()`; thread-safe via `threading.Lock`.
- Ôťů 53B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched ÔÇö `GET /api/v1/breakers`, `POST /api/v1/breakers` (registers a named breaker via `_get_or_create_locked`), `POST /api/v1/breakers/{name}/reset` (registered BEFORE bare `/{name}` GET so the literal `/reset` doesn't get captured), `GET /api/v1/breakers/{name}` (404 if missing) wired into `create_app(circuit_breaker=...)`.

**Phase 64 ÔÇö Complete.** All 146 test modules green. Sovereign Command Bus ÔÇö named handlers register at runtime, dispatch by name with a payload dict; each call produces a `CommandResult` recorded in a ring-buffer history (max 500). Stdlib only:

Sovereign Saga Orchestrator ÔÇö long-running multi-step workflow engine; each step is a named callable that transforms a payload dict, output of step N becomes input of step N+1; on any failure the saga records `status="failed"` with the failing step + error and stops. **Phase 69 ÔÇö Complete.** All 155 test modules green. Sovereign Signal Anomaly Detector ÔÇö z-score statistical outlier detection over a named `SignalAggregator` signal. Downsamples the windowed history into 1-second buckets (the mean of all readings sharing `floor(recorded_at)`) for a sampling-rate-independent baseline, scores the most recent bucket as a z-score against the windowed population mean/stddev, and maps `|z|` to a severity label (`normal` < 2 ÔëĄ `warning` < 3 ÔëĄ `critical`). Pure stdlib ÔÇö no numpy/scipy:

- Ôťů 69A: `pradyos/core/anomaly_detector.py` ÔÇö `_severity(z)` (|z|Ôëą3 Ôćĺ critical, Ôëą2 Ôćĺ warning, else normal); `AnomalyResult(signal, sample_size, window, mean, stddev, latest_value, z_score, severity, computed_at)` dataclass with `to_dict()`; `AnomalyDetector(aggregator)` with `detect(signal, window=3600.0)` (filters points by `recorded_at >= now Ôłĺ window` via the aggregator's public `get()`; 1-second bucketing; `n==0` Ôćĺ all-zero `normal` result; `n<2` Ôćĺ no-spread `normal`; else population stddev + `z=(latest Ôłĺ mean)/stddev`, `0.0` when stddev is 0; mean/stddev/latest/z rounded to 6 dp), `get_cached(signal, window)`, `cache_result(result)` (insertion-order LRU, evicts oldest beyond 128); thread-safe via `threading.Lock`. **Deviation:** the literal Phase 69 brief ("Sovereign Correlation Engine") already shipped as Phase 33, and the previously-planned Circuit Breaker likewise overlapped existing work ÔÇö so Phase 69 delivers a new, non-colliding Anomaly Detector that reuses the Phase 31 `SignalAggregator` without modifying it.
- Ôťů 69B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase69.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged) ÔÇö added `anomaly_detector: Any | None = None` param and 2 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/anomaly?signal=X&window=Y&use_cache=bool` and `POST /api/v1/anomaly` (body `{signal, window?, use_cache?}`); both return `{"error": ...}` when no detector is configured or `signal` is missing, and tag each response with `"cached"` (true only on a `use_cache` hit).
- Ôťů 69C: `tests/test_anomaly_detector.py` ÔÇö 20 unit tests (init; return type; missing-signal zero result; single-bucket/constant no-spread; clear positive + negative anomaly Ôćĺ critical; mean + population stddev; z-score formula; parametrized severity normal/warning/critical bands incl. negative z; 1-second bucketing averages same-second readings; window excludes old points; window value preserved; 6-dp rounding; `to_dict` keys; cache miss/store/retrieve; LRU eviction caps at 128; 30-thread concurrent detect/cache safety).
- Ôťů 69D: `tests/test_anomaly_web.py` ÔÇö 10 FastAPI TestClient tests (no-engine GET/POST errors; valid GET 200 + all fields; valid POST 200; unknown signal Ôćĺ sample_size 0; `use_cache` miss-then-hit; window defaults to 3600.0; window filter excludes old points).
- Ôťů 69E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 155 test modules registered (running total; Phase 69 appends `test_anomaly_detector.py` + `test_anomaly_web.py`).
- Ôťů 69F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 70 planned.

**Phase 70 ÔÇö Complete.** All 157 test modules green. Sovereign Dependency Graph ÔÇö tracks directed dependencies between named components (an edge `a -> b` means "a depends on b"), stored as a forward adjacency map plus a mirror reverse map so both "what does X need?" and "who needs X?" are O(1). Pure stdlib ÔÇö no third-party deps; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- Ôťů 70A: `pradyos/core/dependency_graph.py` ÔÇö `CycleError(cycle)` (carries the offending node path, closed on itself); `DependencyGraph` with `add_dependency(frm, to)` (idempotent, auto-creates nodes), `remove_dependency(frm, to)` (returns whether the edge existed; nodes retained), `get_dependencies(node)` / `get_dependents(node)` (direct, sorted), `impact_score(node)` (count of transitive dependents ÔÇö how far a failure ripples), `find_cycle()` (DFS back-edge search Ôćĺ closed cycle path or `None`), `topological_sort(start=None)` (Kahn's algorithm, dependency-first, alphabetical tie-break for determinism; restricted to a node's transitive closure when `start` is given; raises `CycleError` on cycles), `describe(node)` (JSON snapshot), `has_node` / `nodes`. **Deviation:** the literal Phase 70 brief ("Sovereign Correlation Engine") already shipped as Phase 33 ÔÇö so, following the Phase 69 precedent, Phase 70 delivers a new, non-colliding Dependency Graph; the previously-planned Anomaly Watch is deferred to Phase 71.
- Ôťů 70B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase70.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ÔÇö added `dependency_graph: Any | None = None` param and 5 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/deps/{node}` (node snapshot), `POST /api/v1/deps` (body `{from, to}`; 422 when either is missing), `DELETE /api/v1/deps/{from}/{to}`, `GET /api/v1/deps/{node}/sort` (topo sort from the node; 409 + cycle path on a cycle), and `GET /api/v1/deps/{node}/impact`; all return `{"error": ...}` when no graph is configured.
- Ôťů 70C: `tests/test_dependency_graph.py` ÔÇö 23 unit tests (init; add creates both nodes; dependencies/dependents; idempotent add; remove true/false + node retention; membership; unknown-node empties; linear-chain + edge-respecting + deterministic topo sort; scoped sort from a node; cycle Ôćĺ `CycleError` with a valid path; `find_cycle` none/simple/self-loop; impact score direct + transitive; `describe` fields; 20-thread concurrent-add safety).
- Ôťů 70D: `tests/test_dependency_web.py` ÔÇö 10 FastAPI TestClient tests (no-engine GET/POST errors; node info + fields; POST adds edge; POST missing field Ôćĺ 422; DELETE removes / non-existent Ôćĺ false; topo sort order; cycle Ôćĺ 409 with closed path; impact score).
- Ôťů 70E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 157 test modules registered (running total; Phase 70 appends `test_dependency_graph.py` + `test_dependency_web.py`).

**Phase 71 ÔÇö Complete.** All 159 test modules green. Sovereign Anomaly Watch ÔÇö a real-time anomaly-detection watchdog that polls registered service health metrics and scores the latest reading of each source with a scikit-learn `IsolationForest` (the same algorithm the hardware-intel service uses), flagging statistical outliers; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- Ôťů 71A: `pradyos/core/anomaly_watch.py` ÔÇö `SourceNotFoundError(name)` (carries the offending source name); `AnomalyWatch(min_samples=10, window=256, contamination="auto", n_estimators=100, random_state=42)` with `register_source(name, metric_fn, baseline=None)` (a zero-arg `metric_fn` returns the live metric; the optional `baseline` pre-seeds the rolling window), `tick()` (polls every source, appends its reading to a bounded window, and scores the latest value once Ôëą `min_samples` readings exist ÔÇö returning `{"status": "warming_up"}` before that, and isolating any source whose `metric_fn` raises as `{"status": "error"}` rather than aborting the tick), `get_anomalies()` (latest results currently flagged anomalous), `get_status()` (latest per-source results), `deregister(name)` (raises `SourceNotFoundError`), `sources()` / `has_source()` / `sample_count()`, and `clear()`. **Deviation:** the README's earlier Phase 71 sketch (a z-score `AnomalyDetector` loop over `SignalAggregator`) is superseded by this brief's IsolationForest design; it ships as a new module distinct from the Phase 69 detector, so nothing is overwritten.

These sub-paths coexist with the Phase 69 `GET`/`POST /api/v1/anomaly` z-score routes without shadowing them.

**Phase 72 ÔÇö Complete.** All 161 test modules green. Sovereign Bloom Filter ÔÇö a space-efficient probabilistic set-membership structure: items are hashed into a fixed bit array via KirschÔÇôMitzenmacher double-hashing (two 64-bit halves of one SHA-256 digest), so `contains` may false-positive but **never** false-negatives ÔÇö ideal for cheap "have I seen this?" guards. Pure stdlib (`hashlib` + a `bytearray`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. **Pivot:** the previously-planned Phase 72 "Policy Engine" namespace is fully occupied by Phase 14 (`pradyos/imperium/policy_engine.py`, `/api/v1/policy/rules`, both test modules), and "Event Bus" collided with `pradyos/core/bus.py::EventBus` + the Phase 48 `/api/v1/events` event store ÔÇö so, following the standing pivot precedent, Phase 72 ships a new, namespace-verified Bloom Filter.

- Ôťů 72A: `pradyos/core/bloom_filter.py` ÔÇö `BloomFilter(capacity=1000, error_rate=0.01)` derives the optimal bit count `m = ceil(-(n┬Ěln p)/(ln 2)┬▓)` and hash count `k = round((m/n)┬Ěln 2)`; `add(item) Ôćĺ bool` (True when a new bit was set), `add_many(items) Ôćĺ int` (count newly set), `contains(item)` / `__contains__`, `clear()`, `__len__` (approx distinct added), `fill_ratio()`, `estimated_false_positive_rate()`, `stats()` (JSON snapshot), plus `capacity` / `error_rate` / `bits` / `hashes` properties. Any key type is accepted (strings hashed directly, others via `repr`). Invalid `capacity` / `error_rate` raise `ValueError`.
- Ôťů 72B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase72.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ÔÇö added a `bloom_filter: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/bloom` (stats), `POST /api/v1/bloom/add` (body `{item}` or `{items: [...]}`; 422 on missing/non-string), `GET /api/v1/bloom/contains/{item}`, and `DELETE /api/v1/bloom` (clear); all return `{"error": ...}` when no filter is configured. The `/api/v1/bloom` prefix was verified free against every existing route.
- Ôťů 72C: `tests/test_bloom_filter.py` ÔÇö 26 unit tests (sizing from capacity/error_rate; invalid-arg `ValueError`; add new/dup; contains hit/miss + `in` operator; `add_many` counts; `len`; the no-false-negative guarantee over 500 items; empirical false-positive rate within bound; clear; stats keys/count; fill-ratio; estimated-fpp; property accessors; non-string + unicode keys; 10-thread concurrent-add safety).
- Ôťů 72D: `tests/test_bloom_filter_web.py` ÔÇö 14 FastAPI TestClient tests (no-filter errors on all four routes; stats keys; add single/list; missing / non-string Ôćĺ 422; contains hit/miss; clear resets; no-false-negative over HTTP).
- Ôťů 72E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 161 test modules registered (running total; Phase 72 appends `test_bloom_filter.py` + `test_bloom_filter_web.py`).
- Ôťů 72F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 73 planned.

**Phase 73 ÔÇö Complete.** All 163 test modules green. Sovereign Consistent Hash Ring ÔÇö maps arbitrary keys to a changing set of nodes so that adding or removing a node reshuffles only that node's keys, never the rest (the consistent-hashing property). Each node is placed at `replicas` points around a 2^64 SHA-256 ring; a key is owned by the first node clockwise, located in O(log V) via `bisect`. Pure stdlib (`hashlib` + `bisect`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- Ôťů 73A: `pradyos/core/hash_ring.py` ÔÇö `NodeNotFoundError(node)` (carries the offending name); `HashRing(nodes=None, *, replicas=100)` with `add_node` (idempotent), `remove_node` (raises `NodeNotFoundError`), `get_node(key)` (owner, or `None` on an empty ring), `get_nodes(key, count)` (distinct clockwise nodes for replication), `nodes()` / `has_node()`, `distribution(keys)` (per-node key counts), `stats()` (JSON snapshot), and `clear()`. Invalid `replicas` raises `ValueError`.

**Phase 74 ÔÇö Complete.** All 165 test modules green. Sovereign Cardinality Estimator ÔÇö a HyperLogLog sketch that counts *distinct* items in a stream using fixed memory (m = 2^precision one-byte registers), independent of stream size. Each item is hashed (SHA-1 Ôćĺ 64 bits); the top `precision` bits pick a register, which keeps the largest leading-zero rank seen. The estimate uses the bias-corrected harmonic-mean formula with linear-counting in the small range, for Ôëł1.04/ÔłÜm relative error (~0.8% at precision 14). Pure stdlib (`hashlib` + `math`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- Ôťů 74A: `pradyos/core/hyperloglog.py` ÔÇö `HyperLogLog(precision=14)` with `add(item)` / `add_many(items)`, `estimate()` (rounded distinct count) / `__len__`, `merge(other)` (register-wise max union; raises `ValueError` on precision mismatch or non-HLL), `clear()`, `fill_ratio()`, `stats()` (JSON snapshot), and `precision` / `registers` properties. Any key type is accepted (strings hashed directly, others via `repr`). Invalid `precision` (outside 4ÔÇô16) raises `ValueError`.
- Ôťů 74B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase74.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ÔÇö added a `hyperloglog: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/cardinality` (stats), `POST /api/v1/cardinality/add` (body `{item}` or `{items: [...]}`; 422 on missing/non-string), `GET /api/v1/cardinality/estimate`, and `DELETE /api/v1/cardinality` (clear); all return `{"error": ...}` when no estimator is configured. The `/api/v1/cardinality` prefix was verified free against every existing route.
- Ôťů 74C: `tests/test_hyperloglog.py` ÔÇö 27 unit tests (precision/register sizing + invalid-arg `ValueError`; empty/single/duplicate counts; `__len__`; accuracy within 3% at 1k/10k/50k; determinism; low-precision survival; merge as union / disjoint / identical / commutative + mismatch & non-HLL guards; clear; fill-ratio; stats; non-string + unicode keys; 10-thread concurrency).

**Phase 75 ÔÇö Complete.** All 167 test modules green. Sovereign Vector Clock ÔÇö tracks the causal ordering of events across independent actors. Each actor bumps its own counter on a local event (`tick`); receiving a message folds in the sender's clock via element-wise max (`merge`); comparing two clocks (`compare`) reports `before` / `after` / `equal` / `concurrent` (causally independent ÔÇö a conflict). Missing actors count as 0 so clocks with different actor sets compare cleanly. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- Ôťů 75A: `pradyos/core/vectorclock.py` ÔÇö `VectorClock(initial=None)` with `tick(actor)` (returns the new counter), `merge(other)` (element-wise max; `ValueError` on non-VectorClock), `compare(other)` Ôćĺ `before|after|equal|concurrent`, `get(actor)`, `actors()`, `to_dict()` (copy), `copy()`, `clear()`, and `stats()`. Negative or non-integer initial values raise `ValueError`.
- Ôťů 75B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase75.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ÔÇö added a `vectorclock: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/clocks` (state), `POST /api/v1/clocks/tick` (body `{actor}`; 422 on missing), `POST /api/v1/clocks/merge` (body `{clock}`; 422 on non-dict or bad values), and `POST /api/v1/clocks/compare` (body `{clock}` Ôćĺ `{relation}`); all return `{"error": ...}` when no clock is configured. The `/api/v1/clocks` prefix was verified free against every existing route.

**Phase 76 ÔÇö Complete.** All 169 test modules green. Sovereign Frequency Sketch ÔÇö a Count-Min Sketch that estimates per-item frequencies over a stream in fixed `depth ├Ś width` memory. Each item is hashed into one counter per row via KirschÔÇôMitzenmacher double-hashing (two 64-bit halves of one SHA-256 digest, combined as `(h1 + row┬Ěh2) mod width`); `estimate` is the minimum across rows, so collisions can only inflate it ÔÇö it **never under-counts**. Pure stdlib (`hashlib`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- Ôťů 76A: `pradyos/core/countminsketch.py` ÔÇö `CountMinSketch(width=2000, depth=5)` with `add(item, count=1)` (count must be a positive integer), `estimate(item) Ôćĺ int` (min across rows ÔÇö an upper bound), `merge(other) Ôćĺ CountMinSketch` (element-wise sum into a NEW sketch; neither input mutated; `ValueError` on dimension mismatch or non-sketch), `clear()`, `stats()` (width / depth / cells / total), and `width` / `depth` properties. Invalid `width` / `depth` (ÔëĄ 0) raise `ValueError`.
- Ôťů 76B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase76.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ÔÇö added a `countminsketch: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/frequency` (stats), `POST /api/v1/frequency/add` (body `{item, count=1}`; 422 on missing item or non-positive count), `POST /api/v1/frequency/estimate` (body `{item}`), and `POST /api/v1/frequency/merge` (body `{items: [...], item?}` ÔÇö merges a sketch built from those items with the live one via `merge()` and reports the merged total / estimate); all return `{"error": ...}` when no sketch is configured. Sovereign Merkle Tree ÔÇö hashes an ordered list of items into a single root such that any change to any item flips the root, and membership is provable with an audit path of only ÔîłlogÔéé nÔîë sibling hashes (without revealing the other items). Leaves are SHA-256 of each item; each level hashes adjacent pairs (`H(left || right)`), duplicating the last node on odd levels to stay balanced. Pure stdlib (`hashlib`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- Ôťů 77A: `pradyos/core/merkle_tree.py` ÔÇö `MerkleTree` with `add(item)` (leaf append; `ValueError` on None), `build()` / `root` property (hex root, or `None` when empty), `proof(item)` (audit path of `{"hash", "side"}` entries; `ValueError` if the tree is empty or the item is absent), `verify(item)` (recomputes the root from the item + its proof Ôćĺ bool), `clear()`, `stats()` (leaves / height / root), and `__len__`. Odd-leaf duplication keeps the tree balanced; the proof length is ÔîłlogÔéé nÔîë.
- Ôťů 77B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase77.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ÔÇö added a `merkle_tree: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/merkle` (stats), `POST /api/v1/merkle/add` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing), `POST /api/v1/merkle/verify` (body `{item}` Ôćĺ `{verified}`), and `POST /api/v1/merkle/proof` (body `{item}` Ôćĺ audit path + root; 404 when the item isn't a leaf); all return `{"error": ...}` when no tree is configured. The `/api/v1/merkle` prefix was verified free.

**Phase 79 ÔÇö Complete.** All 175 test modules green. Sovereign T-Digest ÔÇö estimates streaming quantiles (median, p95, p99 ÔÇŽ) in compact, mergeable memory. **Phase 80 ÔÇö Complete.** All 177 test modules green. Sovereign Fenwick Tree ÔÇö a binary indexed tree answering prefix-sum queries and point updates both in O(log n) by exploiting the binary structure of indices (each slot covers a range of length `i & -i`; updates walk up by adding that bit, prefix sums walk down by subtracting it). 1-indexed; `range_sum(lo, hi) = prefix_sum(hi) - prefix_sum(lo-1)`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- Ôťů 80A: `pradyos/core/fenwick.py` ÔÇö `FenwickTree(size)` with `update(i, delta)` (1-indexed; int or float, may be negative), `prefix_sum(i)` (sum of 1..i; `prefix_sum(0)=0`), `range_sum(lo, hi)` (inclusive), `point_query(i)` (value at i), `resize(new_size)` (preserves the overlap), `clear()`, `size` property, and `stats()` (size / total). Out-of-bounds indices, `lo > hi`, non-integer indices, non-numeric deltas, and `size < 1` raise `ValueError`.
- Ôťů 80B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase80.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ÔÇö added a `fenwick: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/fenwick` (stats), `POST /api/v1/fenwick/update` (body `{index, delta}`), `POST /api/v1/fenwick/query` (body `{lo, hi}` Ôćĺ range sum), and `POST /api/v1/fenwick/point` (body `{index}` Ôćĺ value); invalid input maps the core's `ValueError` to 422; all return `{"error": ...}` when no tree is configured. The `/api/v1/fenwick` prefix was verified free.

**Phase 81 ÔÇö Complete.** All 179 test modules green. Sovereign Segment Tree ÔÇö O(log n) range queries (sum / min / max, fixed at construction) with point updates over a fixed-size array, more general than a Fenwick tree. Implemented as an iterative bottom-up tree (a flat `2┬Ěn` array, leaves in `[n, 2n)`) for cache-friendly speed; sum/min/max are commutative + associative so the bottom-up combine order is correct. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- Ôťů 81A: `pradyos/core/segtree.py` ÔÇö `SegmentTree(size, mode='sum')` (mode Ôłł sum/min/max) with `update(i, val)` (1-indexed point *set*; int/float, may be negative), `query(lo, hi)` (inclusive range aggregate), `point_query(i)`, `resize(new_size)` (preserves the overlap, clears the extension), `clear()`, `size` / `mode` properties, and `stats()` (size / mode / aggregate). Invalid size, invalid mode, out-of-bounds indices, `lo > hi`, and non-numeric values raise `ValueError`. **Note:** uses the iterative `2┬Ěn` layout rather than the textbook recursive `4┬Ěn` because recursive Python missed the O(log n) latency budget on n=1M (Ôëł0.14 s vs Ôëł0.08 s).
- Ôťů 81B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase81.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ÔÇö added a `segtree: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/segtree` (stats), `POST /api/v1/segtree/update` (body `{index, value}`), `POST /api/v1/segtree/query` (body `{lo, hi}` Ôćĺ `{mode, result}`), and `POST /api/v1/segtree/point` (body `{index}` Ôćĺ value); invalid input maps the core's `ValueError` to 422; all return `{"error": ...}` when no tree is configured. The `/api/v1/segtree` prefix was verified free.

- Ôťů 81D: `tests/test_segtree_web.py` ÔÇö 18 FastAPI TestClient tests (no-tree errors on all four routes; stats keys + mode; update reflected / out-of-bounds Ôćĺ 422 / bad value Ôćĺ 422; query in sum / min / max modes / boundary / out-of-bounds Ôćĺ 422 / lo>hi Ôćĺ 422; point value / out-of-bounds Ôćĺ 422; round-trip; plus a regression check that the Phase 77ÔÇô80 routes are still live).

**Phase 82 ÔÇö Complete.** All 181 test modules green. Sovereign Union-Find ÔÇö a disjoint-set forest tracking a partition of n elements with effectively constant-time connectivity queries. Union by rank keeps trees shallow and path-halving `find` flattens them as a side effect of the query, giving the near-O(╬▒(n)) bound (╬▒ ÔëĄ 4 for any practical n). 1-indexed. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- Ôťů 82A: `pradyos/core/unionfind.py` ÔÇö `UnionFind(size)` with `union(a, b)` (returns whether a merge happened; a self-union or an already-connected union is a no-op), `find(a)` (iterative path halving), `connected(a, b)`, `component_size(a)`, `component_count()`, `reset()`, `size` property, and `stats()` (size / components / largest_component). Out-of-bounds and non-integer elements raise `ValueError`. Rank (a height bound) drives unions; element counts are tracked separately for `component_size`.
- Ôťů 82B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase82.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ÔÇö added a `unionfind: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/unionfind` (stats), `POST /api/v1/unionfind/union` (body `{a, b}` Ôćĺ `{united, components}`), `POST /api/v1/unionfind/find` (body `{a}` Ôćĺ `{root, component_size}`), and `POST /api/v1/unionfind/connected` (body `{a, b}` Ôćĺ `{connected}`); invalid input maps the core's `ValueError` to 422; all return `{"error": ...}` when no structure is configured. The `/api/v1/unionfind` prefix was verified free.

Sovereign Trie ÔÇö a prefix tree mapping string keys to values: O(len(key)) insert / search / delete and an O(len(prefix) + matches) prefix scan (the primitive behind autocomplete and namespace lookups). Traversals are iterative (explicit stack) so a pathologically long key can never blow the recursion limit; deleting a key prunes its dangling node chain. **Phase 84 ÔÇö Complete.** All 185 test modules green. Sovereign LRU Cache ÔÇö a fixed-capacity keyÔćĺvalue cache with least-recently-used eviction and optional per-key TTL. The clock is injectable for deterministic TTL tests. Invalid capacity / ttl / key raise `ValueError`.

**Phase 85 ÔÇö Complete.** All 187 test modules green. Sovereign Reservoir Sampler ÔÇö draws a statistically uniform random sample of fixed size k from a stream of unknown length in O(k) memory and one pass (Vitter's Algorithm R): the first k items fill the reservoir, then the i-th item replaces a uniformly chosen slot with probability k/(i+1), so every item seen is equally likely (k/n) to be retained. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/reservoir_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 85A: `pradyos/core/reservoir.py` ÔÇö `ReservoirError(capacity)`; `SovereignReservoir(k, random_fn=random.random)` with `feed(item)` (Algorithm R step), `feed_many(items)`, `sample()` (copy; unordered, ÔëĄ k), `reset(k=None)` (clear / resize), `__len__`, `capacity` / `seen` properties, and `stats()` (capacity / seen / filled). The RNG is injectable (zero-arg Ôćĺ float in [0,1)) for deterministic tests. Invalid capacity raises `ReservoirError`.
- Ôťů 85B: `pradyos/web/reservoir_web.py` ÔÇö `register_reservoir_routes(app, reservoir=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sampler, k=16) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/reservoir/feed` (body `{item}` or `{items: [...]}`; 422 on neither), `GET /api/v1/reservoir/sample`, `POST /api/v1/reservoir/reset` (body `{capacity?}`; 422 on bad capacity), `GET /api/v1/reservoir/stats`.
- Ôťů 85C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase85.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `reservoir` param, and a single `register_reservoir_routes(app, reservoir)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 86 ÔÇö Complete.** All 189 test modules green. Sovereign Cuckoo Filter ÔÇö a probabilistic set-membership structure like the Phase 72 Bloom filter but supporting **deletion**. Each item is reduced to a small fingerprint stored in one of two candidate buckets via partial-key cuckoo hashing (`i1 = h(item) mod m`, `i2 = i1 XOR (h(fp) mod m)`); when both are full an existing fingerprint is "kicked" to its alternate bucket and the cascade repeats up to `max_kicks` times. A failed insert is rolled back atomically, so `contains` may false-positive (Ôëł `2┬Ěbucket_size / 2^fp_bits`) but **never** false-negatives a present item. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/cuckoo_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 86A: `pradyos/core/cuckoo.py` ÔÇö `CuckooError(detail)`; `SovereignCuckooFilter(capacity, bucket_size=4, fingerprint_bits=8, max_kicks=500, hash_fn=None)` with `insert(item)` Ôćĺ bool (False if full after `max_kicks`; rolls back the kick cascade on failure Ôćĺ no false negatives), `contains(item)` Ôćĺ bool, `delete(item)` Ôćĺ bool (False if absent), `reset()`, `__contains__`, `__len__`, `capacity` property, and `stats()` (capacity / count / load_factor / fingerprint_bits / max_kicks). Bucket count rounds up to a power of two so the XOR alternate-index is a clean involution; the hash is injectable for deterministic tests. Invalid config raises `CuckooError`.
- Ôťů 86B: `pradyos/web/cuckoo_web.py` ÔÇö `register_cuckoo_routes(app, cuckoo=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter, capacity 1024) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/cuckoo/insert` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing), `POST /api/v1/cuckoo/contains`, `DELETE /api/v1/cuckoo/delete` (body `{item}`), `GET /api/v1/cuckoo/stats`, `POST /api/v1/cuckoo/reset`.
- Ôťů 86C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase86.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `cuckoo` param, and a single `register_cuckoo_routes(app, cuckoo)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 86D: `tests/test_cuckoo.py` (43) + `tests/test_cuckoo_web.py` (19) ÔÇö insert / contains / delete correctness; delete-absent Ôćĺ False; re-insert after delete; no-false-negative guarantee under saturation (rollback); injected-hash false positives + their clearing on delete; power-of-two capacity rounding + config validation / `CuckooError` (incl. `bool` rejection); load-factor tracking; full-filter max-kicks behaviour (single-bucket constant hash); seeded false-positive-rate bound + wider-fingerprint comparison; 10-thread concurrency + concurrent insert/delete; all 5 endpoints incl. deterministic membership-with-deletion over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- Ôťů 86E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 189 test modules registered (Phase 86 appends `test_cuckoo.py` + `test_cuckoo_web.py`).

**Phase 87 ÔÇö Complete.** All 191 test modules green. Sovereign Top-K (Space-Saving) ÔÇö a streaming heavy-hitters sketch that tracks the approximate `k` most frequent items in **bounded O(k) memory** regardless of stream length (MetwallyÔÇôAgrawal Space-Saving). At most `k` (item Ôćĺ count, error) entries are monitored; a monitored item increments, an unmonitored one is admitted while fewer than `k` are tracked, and once full the **minimum-count** entry is evicted and reassigned to the new item (its count becomes `min_count + 1`, its error the evicted `min_count`). Because every step keeps the invariant `sum(counts) == total`, the minimum count is ÔëĄ `n/k` when full ÔÇö giving the **heavy-hitter guarantee** (any item with true frequency > `n/k` is always monitored) and the **error bound** (a reported count over-estimates by at most its error ÔëĄ `n/k`). Where Phase 76's Count-Min Sketch answers point queries ("how often did X appear?"), this answers ranking ("what are the top K?") ÔÇö together the complete approximate-frequency stack. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/topk_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 87A: `pradyos/core/space_saving.py` ÔÇö `SpaceSavingError(detail)`; `SpaceSaving(k=10)` with `add(item)` / `add_many(items)` (items must be hashable; raises `TypeError` *before* mutating, so the sum-invariant survives a bad item), `count(item)` / `error(item)` (0 if unmonitored), `top(n=None)` (descending by count, ties keep first-monitored order), `reset(k=None)` (clear / resize), `__len__`, `__contains__`, `k` / `total` properties, and `stats()` (k / monitored / total / min_count). Invalid `k` raises `SpaceSavingError`.
- Ôťů 87B: `pradyos/web/topk_web.py` ÔÇö `register_topk_routes(app, space_saving=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, k=10) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/topk/insert` (body `{item}` or `{items: [...]}`; 422 on neither / non-list / unhashable), `GET /api/v1/topk/query` (`?n=N`, `Query(ge=0)` Ôćĺ 422 on negative / non-int; omit N for all), `GET /api/v1/topk/stats`, `POST /api/v1/topk/reset` (body `{k?}`; 422 on bad k).
- Ôťů 87C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase87.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `space_saving` param, and a single `register_topk_routes(app, space_saving)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 87D: `tests/test_space_saving.py` (44) + `tests/test_topk_web.py` (20) ÔÇö add / count / `add_many`; deterministic eviction (k=2 : a,b,a,c Ôćĺ b evicted, c carries error 1); exact-before-eviction (error 0); top ordering / `n`-slicing / tie order / structure; heavy-hitter guarantee + correct ranking on a seeded skewed stream; `sum(counts) == total` invariant (incl. under 8-thread contention with eviction); error bound `est Ôłĺ true ÔëĄ error ÔëĄ min_count`; k validation / `SpaceSavingError` (incl. `bool` & `float` rejection); stats / reset / resize; integer & mixed hashable items; unhashable-without-corruption; 10-thread concurrency; all 4 endpoints incl. deterministic eviction over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- Ôťů 87E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 191 test modules registered (Phase 87 appends `test_space_saving.py` + `test_topk_web.py`).
- Ôťů 87F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 88 planned.

**Phase 88 ÔÇö Complete.** All 193 test modules green. Sovereign MinHash ÔÇö estimates the **Jaccard similarity** `|AÔłęB| / |AÔł¬B|` of two sets in compact O(num_hashes) space, never storing raw members. For each of `num_hashes` universal hash functions it keeps, per named set, the *minimum* hashed value across that set's members (its "signature"); since `P[min_i(A) == min_i(B)] == Jaccard(A,B)`, the **fraction of signature positions where two sets agree is an unbiased estimate of their Jaccard similarity** (variance ÔłŁ 1/num_hashes). The hash family is `h_i(x) = (a_i┬Ěx + b_i) mod p` with `p = 2**61Ôłĺ1` and coefficients seeded once at init (deterministic given a fixed `seed`); members fold to a stable BLAKE2b integer so determinism holds across processes. Where Phase 74's HyperLogLog estimates *cardinality* and Phases 76/87 estimate *frequency*, this estimates set *similarity* ÔÇö the Jaccard third of the sketch stack. A deliberate deviation from a loosely-sketched `ÔÇŽmod p mod num_hashes`: that final reduction collapses every hash into `[0, num_hashes)` and inflates all estimates toward 1.0 (empirically est 0.78 vs true 0.16), so the standard full-range construction is used. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/minhash_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 88A: `pradyos/core/minhash.py` ÔÇö `MinHashError(detail)`; `MinHash(num_hashes=128, seed=0)` is a multi-set store (shared hash family + one signature per named set) with `add(set, element)` / `add_many(set, elements)`, `similarity(a, b)` Ôćĺ Jaccard estimate (0.0 if either set is unknown), `signature(set)` (copy or None), `sets()`, `reset(num_hashes=None, seed=None)` (clear / reconfigure), `__len__`, `__contains__`, `num_hashes` / `seed` properties, and `stats()` (num_hashes / sets / total_added / seed). Invalid `num_hashes` or `seed` raises `MinHashError`.
- Ôťů 88B: `pradyos/web/minhash_web.py` ÔÇö `register_minhash_routes(app, minhash=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app store, num_hashes=128) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/minhash/add` (body `{set, element}` or `{set, elements: [...]}`; 422 on missing set / neither / non-list), `GET /api/v1/minhash/similarity` (`?a=&b=`, required Ôćĺ 422 if absent), `GET /api/v1/minhash/stats`, `POST /api/v1/minhash/reset` (body `{num_hashes?, seed?}`; 422 on bad num_hashes).
- Ôťů 88C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase88.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `minhash` param, and a single `register_minhash_routes(app, minhash)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 88D: `tests/test_minhash.py` (44) + `tests/test_minhash_web.py` (20) ÔÇö add / signature / sets; self-similarity = 1.0, identical-content = 1.0, disjoint Ôëł 0, missing-set = 0.0, symmetry; seeded accuracy (mean |error| < 0.05 at 256 hashes) + a 1/3-Jaccard estimate within 0.08; determinism + order-independence + idempotent re-add; the sum-of-minima monotone-non-increasing invariant + element-wise-min lowering + values within `2**61Ôłĺ1`; `num_hashes` / `seed` validation / `MinHashError` (incl. `bool` & `float` rejection, negative seed allowed); stats / reset / reconfigure; mixed element types; 10-thread concurrency + a same-set order-independent signature check; all 4 endpoints incl. deterministic Jaccard over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- Ôťů 88E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 193 test modules registered (Phase 88 appends `test_minhash.py` + `test_minhash_web.py`).
- Ôťů 88F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 89 planned.

**Phase 89 ÔÇö Complete.** All 195 test modules green. Sovereign SimHash ÔÇö locality-sensitive fingerprints for **near-duplicate detection** (Charikar). A document (a bag of feature tokens) folds to a single `num_bits` integer: for every token we take a stable hash and, per bit position, cast a weighted vote (+1 if that bit of the token hash is set, Ôłĺ1 otherwise); summing the votes over all tokens and thresholding at zero yields the fingerprint. Because votes are summed, it is a **bag-of-words** signature ÔÇö token order is irrelevant, token frequency is not. The **Hamming distance** (popcount of the XOR) between two fingerprints measures dissimilarity: identical documents share every bit (distance 0), near-duplicates differ in only a handful of bits, and unrelated documents sit near `num_bits/2`; the normalized similarity is `1 Ôłĺ hamming/num_bits`. At 64 bits a Hamming distance ÔëĄ `NEAR_DUPLICATE_HAMMING` (= 3, a documented module constant) is the conventional near-duplicate cutoff (Manku et al.). The token hash mixes in a `seed` (deterministic yet injectable) and uses BLAKE2b ÔÇö not the salted built-in `hash` ÔÇö so fingerprints reproduce across processes. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/simhash_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 89A: `pradyos/core/simhash.py` ÔÇö `SimHashError(detail)` + `NEAR_DUPLICATE_HAMMING = 3`; `SimHash(num_bits=64, seed=0)` is a multi-document store with `hash(doc, tokens)` Ôćĺ fingerprint int (stored), `fingerprint(doc)` (or None), `hamming(a, b)` / `similarity(a, b)` / `near_duplicate(a, b, threshold=3)` (all None if either doc is unknown), `documents()`, `reset(num_bits=None, seed=None)` (clear / reconfigure), `__len__`, `__contains__`, `num_bits` / `seed` properties, and `stats()` (num_bits / docs / total_hashed / seed). Invalid `num_bits` (ÔëĄ0 or >512) or non-int `seed` raises `SimHashError`.
- Ôťů 89B: `pradyos/web/simhash_web.py` ÔÇö `register_simhash_routes(app, simhash=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app store, num_bits=64) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/simhash/hash` (body `{doc, tokens: [...]}`; 422 on missing doc / non-list tokens), `GET /api/v1/simhash/similarity` (`?a=&b=`, required Ôćĺ 422 if absent, 404 on unknown doc), `GET /api/v1/simhash/hamming` (adds a `near_duplicate` flag; 404 on unknown doc), `GET /api/v1/simhash/stats`, `POST /api/v1/simhash/reset` (body `{num_bits?, seed?}`; 422 on bad num_bits).
- Ôťů 89C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase89.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `simhash` param, and a single `register_simhash_routes(app, simhash)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 89D: `tests/test_simhash.py` (50) + `tests/test_simhash_web.py` (22) ÔÇö hash / fingerprint / documents; identical Ôćĺ Hamming 0 & similarity 1.0; 1ÔÇô2 token-swap near-duplicates ÔëĄ 3 bits (on 600-token docs) + `near_duplicate` flag; unrelated docs Ôëł num_bits/2; `similarity == 1 Ôłĺ hamming/num_bits`, symmetry; missing-doc Ôćĺ None / 404; determinism + order-independence + frequency-sensitivity; empty-doc fingerprint 0; `num_bits` (incl. >512) / `seed` validation / `SimHashError` (bool & float rejection, negative seed allowed); custom 128-bit fingerprints; stats / reset / reconfigure; 10-thread concurrency + a same-doc consistent-fingerprint check; all 5 endpoints incl. deterministic near-duplicate over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 90 ÔÇö Complete.** All 197 test modules green. Sovereign Quotient Filter ÔÇö a cache-friendly approximate-membership structure (Bender et al., "Don't Thrash") that, unlike the Phase 72 Bloom filter, supports **exact deletion, duplicate counting, and merging**. Each item folds to a `q + r` bit fingerprint, split into a *quotient* `fq = fp >> r` (the canonical slot, one of `2**q`) and a *remainder* `fr = fp & (2**r Ôłĺ 1)` (stored in the slot). Collisions are resolved by linear probing, with three metadata bits per slot ÔÇö `is_occupied`, `is_continuation`, `is_shifted` ÔÇö that keep every quotient's remainders in one contiguous sorted *run* and group overlapping runs into *clusters*; those bits alone drive run/cluster navigation (no quotient is stored ÔÇö that is the space win). Deletion is exact (no false negatives), duplicates are counted natively, and a membership test false-*positives* with probability `Ôëł 2**(-r)`. Pure stdlib; the hash is injectable for deterministic tests; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/quotient_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 90A: `pradyos/core/quotient.py` ÔÇö `QuotientError(detail)`; `QuotientFilter(q=8, r=8, seed=0, hash_fn=None)` with `insert(item)` Ôćĺ bool (False only when full), `contains(item)` Ôćĺ bool, `count(item)` Ôćĺ int, `delete(item)` Ôćĺ bool (exact; decrements the duplicate count, contracting the cluster when it hits 0), `merge(other)` (same `q`/`r`), `reset(q=None, r=None, seed=None)`, `__contains__`, `__len__`, `q` / `remainder_bits` / `slots` properties, and `stats()` (q / slots / remainder_bits / used / items / load_factor / `false_positive_rate = 2**-r`). Invalid config raises `QuotientError`. The canonical Bender et al. insert/delete maintain the three metadata bits and reconstruct shifted-bits on delete via run-by-run quotient tracking.
- Ôťů 90B: `pradyos/web/quotient_web.py` ÔÇö `register_quotient_routes(app, quotient=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter, q=10 Ôćĺ 1024 slots) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/quotient/insert` (body `{item}`; returns count), `POST /api/v1/quotient/contains` (returns count), `DELETE /api/v1/quotient/delete` (body `{item}`), `GET /api/v1/quotient/stats`, `POST /api/v1/quotient/reset` (body `{q?, r?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config). 422 on missing item.
- Ôťů 90C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase90.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `quotient` param, and a single `register_quotient_routes(app, quotient)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 91 ÔÇö Complete.** All 199 test modules green. Sovereign GK Quantile Sketch (GreenwaldÔÇôKhanna, 2001) ÔÇö streaming **╬Á-approximate quantiles** (p50/p95/p99) over an unbounded stream in `O((1/╬Á)┬Ělog(╬Án))` space, with a hard guarantee: the value returned for a quantile `¤ć` has true rank within `┬▒Ôîł╬ÁnÔîë` of the requested rank. The summary is a value-sorted list of tuples `(v, g, ╬ö)` where `g = r_min(v_i) Ôłĺ r_min(v_{iÔłĺ1})` (so `r_min(v_i) = ╬ú g_j`) and `╬ö = r_max(v_i) Ôłĺ r_min(v_i)`; the invariant `g_i + ╬ö_i ÔëĄ ÔîŐ2╬ÁnÔîő` is what bounds the error. **Insert** places `v` in sorted order with `g = 1`, `╬ö = ÔîŐ2╬ÁnÔîő` (new min/max get `╬ö = 0` ÔÇö exact extremes). **Compress** (every `ÔîŐ1/2╬ÁÔîő` inserts) merges an adjacent pair when `g_i + g_{i+1} + ╬ö_{i+1} ÔëĄ ÔîŐ2╬ÁnÔîő`, which preserves the invariant. **Query** for rank `r = Ôîł¤ćnÔîë` returns the first `v` whose running `r_min` exceeds `r Ôłĺ ╬Án`; the invariant then guarantees `r_max ÔëĄ r + ╬Án`. GK is deterministic by construction (`seed` is accepted for parity). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/gk_quantile_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 91A: `pradyos/core/gk_quantile.py` ÔÇö `GKError(detail)`; `GKSummary(epsilon=0.01, seed=0)` with `insert(value)` / `insert_many(values)` (numbers only), `query(phi)` Ôćĺ ¤ć-quantile (None if empty; `GKError` on `¤ćÔłë[0,1]`), `count()`, `compress()`, `reset(epsilon=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `epsilon` / `seed` / `summary_size` properties, and `stats()` (epsilon / n / summary_size / capacity = `(1/2╬Á)┬Ělog2(2╬Án)`). Invalid `epsilon` (Ôłë(0,1)) / `seed` / value / `phi` raise `GKError`.
- Ôťů 91B: `pradyos/web/gk_quantile_web.py` ÔÇö `register_gk_quantile_routes(app, gk=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app summary, ╬Á=0.01) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/quantile/insert` (body `{value}` or `{values: [...]}`; 422 on neither / non-list / non-number), `GET /api/v1/quantile/query` (`?phi=`, `Query(ge=0.0, le=1.0)` Ôćĺ 422 on ¤ćÔłë[0,1]; **422 on empty summary**), `GET /api/v1/quantile/count`, `GET /api/v1/quantile/stats`, `POST /api/v1/quantile/reset` (body `{epsilon?, seed?}`; 422 on bad epsilon).
- Ôťů 91C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase91.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `gk_quantile` param, and a single `register_gk_quantile_routes(app, gk_quantile)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 92 ÔÇö Complete.** All 201 test modules green. Sovereign KLL Sketch (KarninÔÇôLangÔÇôLiberty, 2016) ÔÇö a randomized, space-optimal, natively **mergeable** streaming-quantile sketch. It maintains a hierarchy of *compactors* (one list per level `h`); an item stored at level `h` carries weight `2**h`. New items enter level 0; when a compactor reaches capacity `k` it **compacts** ÔÇö sort, randomly keep the even- or odd-indexed half (a fair coin discards one of each adjacent pair), and promote the survivors up a level. Each compaction conserves total weight, so `╬ú 2**h == n` always holds; compaction bounds total stored size to `O(k┬Ělog(n/k))` while levels grow as `O(log(n/k))`, giving `O(n/k)` rank error with high probability. **Query** flattens every stored item with its weight, sorts, and returns the weighted-rank `Ôîł¤ćnÔîë` value. **Merge** ÔÇö the defining advantage over Phase 91's GK ÔÇö aligns two sketches level-by-level, concatenates the compactors, and re-compacts, combining distributed sketches with the same guarantee. Randomness is per-*compaction* (a `random.Random(seed)` advancing each compaction), so a fixed insert sequence is deterministic. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/kll_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 92A: `pradyos/core/kll_sketch.py` ÔÇö `KLLError(detail)`; `KLLSketch(k=200, seed=0)` with `update(value)` / `update_many(values)`, `query(phi)` Ôćĺ ¤ć-quantile (None if empty; `KLLError` on ¤ćÔłë[0,1]), `rank(value)` (weighted), `merge(other)` (level-aligned re-compaction), `count()`, `reset(k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `k` / `seed` / `num_levels` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / num_levels / num_compactors / sketch_size_ratio). Invalid `k` (<2) / `seed` / value / `phi` raise `KLLError`. (Uniform per-level capacity `k`: a starved top compactor would let a few heavy items skew the estimate, so every weight keeps a full-resolution buffer ÔÇö measured ratio Ôëł 0.03 at n=10k.)
- Ôťů 92B: `pradyos/web/kll_sketch_web.py` ÔÇö `register_kll_sketch_routes(app, kll=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, k=200) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/kll/insert` (body `{value}` or `{values: [...]}`; 422 on neither / non-list / non-number), `GET /api/v1/kll/query` (`?phi=`, `Query(ge=0.0, le=1.0)`; **422 on empty sketch**), `POST /api/v1/kll/merge` (body `{values: [...]}` Ôćĺ builds a temp sketch and merges it in), `GET /api/v1/kll/stats`, `POST /api/v1/kll/reset` (body `{k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad k).
- Ôťů 92C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase92.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `kll` param, and a single `register_kll_sketch_routes(app, kll)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 92D: `tests/test_kll_sketch.py` (45) + `tests/test_kll_sketch_web.py` (24) ÔÇö update / count / query; rank-error guarantee ÔÇö every p0ÔÇôp100 (incl. extremes) within `3n/k` on uniform and adversarial sorted streams; monotonicity; weighted `rank()` bounds; **merge** (median accuracy, count combination, preserved rank error, empty-into-populated, non-sketch Ôćĺ `KLLError`); space ratio < 0.1 + level growth + the `╬ú weights == n` invariant; determinism (same seed Ôćĺ identical levels); k (<2) / seed / value / phi validation + `KLLError`; stats / reset / reconfigure; duplicate & negative values; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. the merge endpoint + empty Ôćĺ 422 + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 93 ÔÇö Complete.** All 203 test modules green. Sovereign Theta Sketch (K-Minimum-Values) ÔÇö distinct-count (cardinality) estimation that, unlike Phase 74's HyperLogLog, supports a **lossless set union** of two sketches. Each element is hashed uniformly into `[0, 1)`; the sketch retains the `k` smallest *distinct* hashes. Once `k` distinct hashes are retained, `╬Ş` is the largest of them (the `k`-th smallest), so `estimate = (k Ôłĺ 1) / ╬Ş`; below the threshold the retained count is the exact distinct count. Duplicates hash to an already-retained value and are ignored ÔÇö repeats never inflate the count. Relative error is `Ôëł 1/ÔłÜ(kÔłĺ1)` (Ôëł 1.6 % at `k = 4096`). **Union** keeps the `k` smallest hashes of the two retained sets (itself a valid KMV sketch of `A Ôł¬ B`); **intersection** follows by inclusionÔÇôexclusion `|A Ôłę B| Ôëł est(A) + est(B) Ôłĺ est(A Ôł¬ B)`. The BLAKE2b hash is seeded for determinism. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/theta_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 93A: `pradyos/core/theta_sketch.py` ÔÇö `ThetaError(detail)`; `ThetaSketch(k=4096, seed=0)` with `update(element)` / `update_many(elements)`, `estimate()` (0 when empty; exact int below `k`), `merge(other)` (mutating union), `union_estimate(other)` / `intersection_estimate(other)` (non-destructive), `reset(k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `k` / `seed` / `retained_count` / `is_exact` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / theta / retained_count / is_exact / estimate). A max-heap of retained hashes gives O(log k) eviction; a set gives O(1) dedup. Invalid `k` (<2) / `seed` raise `ThetaError`.
- Ôťů 93B: `pradyos/web/theta_sketch_web.py` ÔÇö `register_theta_sketch_routes(app, theta=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, k=4096) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/theta/insert` (body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`; 422 on neither / non-list), `GET /api/v1/theta/estimate` (**0 when empty ÔÇö never 422**), `POST /api/v1/theta/merge` (`?op=union|intersection`, default union ÔÇö union mutates & returns `|AÔł¬B|`, intersection is non-destructive & returns `|AÔłęB|`; 422 on bad op / missing values), `GET /api/v1/theta/stats`, `POST /api/v1/theta/reset` (body `{k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad k).
- Ôťů 93C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase93.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `theta` param, and a single `register_theta_sketch_routes(app, theta)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 93D: `tests/test_theta_sketch.py` (45) + `tests/test_theta_sketch_web.py` (24) ÔÇö 10k-distinct estimate within 5 %; duplicates Ôćĺ exactly 1; exact regime below `k` (estimate == count, `is_exact`); larger-`k` tighter error; **union** (no-overlap Ôćĺ ~2├Ś, full-overlap Ôćĺ ~1├Ś, non-destructive `union_estimate`, count combination, empty/populated edges); **intersection** by inclusionÔÇôexclusion (2500-overlap within 10 %, disjoint Ôëł 0, full overlap); ╬Ş = 1.0 below `k` / <1 when full; retained-count caps at `k`; determinism (same seed Ôćĺ identical retained set) ; k (<2) / seed validation + `ThetaError`; stats / reset / reconfigure; integer elements; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. `op=union|intersection` (incl. non-destructive intersection) + a prior-phase regression check.
